def read_bid_history():
    bid_history = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    bid_history.append({
                        'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'auction_name': parts[2],
                        'bidder_name': parts[3],
                        'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                        'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                    })
    return bid_history


def read_trending():
    trending = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'trending.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    trending.append({
                        'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'item_name': parts[1],
                        'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                        'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                        'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                        'time_period': parts[5]
                    })
    return trending


# Route implementations

@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    auctions = read_auctions()
    trending = read_trending()

    # featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}
    # We define featured as top 5 auctions by current_bid descending and status active
    featured_auctions = [
        {
            'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
            'item_name': auc['item_name'],
            'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
            'end_time': auc['end_time'],
            'image_url': auc['image_url']
        }
        for auc in auctions if auc['status'] == 'Active'
    ]
    featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['current_bid'], reverse=True)
    featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:5]

    # trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}
    # Filter trending for a general period or latest, for simplicity take all times
    trending_auctions = [
        {
            'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
            'item_name': t['item_name'],
            'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
            'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
            'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
        }
        for t in trending
    ]

    return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions)


@app.route('/catalog')
def auction_catalog():
    auctions = read_auctions()
    categories = read_categories()

    # auctions context list with all fields needed
    auctions_ctx = [
        {
            'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
            'item_name': auc['item_name'],
            'description': auc['description'],
            'category': auc['category'],
            'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
            'end_time': auc['end_time'],
            'image_url': auc['image_url']
        }
        for auc in auctions
    ]

    # categories list of strings for filter
    categories_list = [cat['category_name'] for cat in categories]

    return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_ctx, categories=categories_list)


@app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
def auction_details(auction_id):
    auctions = read_auctions()
    bid_history = read_bid_history()

    auction = None
    for auc in auctions:
        if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = {
                'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                'description': auc['description'],
                'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                'status': auc['status'],
                'image_url': auc['image_url']
            }
            break

    if auction is None:
        return "Auction not found", 404

    bid_history_list = [
        {
            'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
            'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
            'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
        }
        for bh in bid_history if bh['auction_id'] == auction_id
    ]

    return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history_list)


@app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
def place_bid(auction_id):
    auctions = read_auctions()
    auction = None
    for auc in auctions:
        if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = {
                'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
            }
            break

    if auction is None:
        return "Auction not found", 404

    return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)


from datetime import datetime

@app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
def submit_bid(auction_id):
    bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder-name', '').strip()
    bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid-amount', '').strip()

    # Validate inputs minimally
    if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
        error_msg = 'Bidder name and bid amount are required.'
        auctions = read_auctions()
        auction = None
        for auc in auctions:
            if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                auction = {
                    'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                    'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                    'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                }
                break
        return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)

    try:
        bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
    except ValueError:
        error_msg = 'Bid amount must be a valid number.'
        auctions = read_auctions()
        auction = None
        for auc in auctions:
            if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                auction = {
                    'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                    'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                    'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                }
                break
        return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)

    auctions = read_auctions()
    auction = None
    for auc in auctions:
        if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = auc
            break

    if auction is None:
        return "Auction not found", 404

    minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid'])
    if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:
        error_msg = f'Bid amount must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid:.2f}).'
        auction_ctx = {
            'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
            'item_name': auction['item_name'],
            'minimum_bid': minimum_bid
        }
        return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_ctx, error=error_msg)

    # Add new bid
    bids = read_bids()
    next_bid_id = 1
    if bids:
        next_bid_id = max(bid['bid_id'] for bid in bids) + 1

    now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')

    new_bid = {
        'bid_id': next_bid_id,
        'auction_id': auction_id,
        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
        'bid_timestamp': now_str
    }
    bids.append(new_bid)
    save_bids(bids)

    # Update auction current bid
    auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount
    save_auctions(auctions)

    # Also update bid_history.txt
    bid_history = read_bid_history()
    next_history_id = 1
    if bid_history:
        next_history_id = max(bh['history_id'] for bh in bid_history) + 1

    new_bid_history = {
        'history_id': next_history_id,
        'auction_id': auction_id,
        'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
        'bid_timestamp': now_str
    }
    bid_history.append(new_bid_history)
    path_bid_hist = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
    with open(path_bid_hist, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for bh in bid_history:
            line = '|'.join([
                str(bh['history_id']),
                str(bh['auction_id']),
                bh['auction_name'],
                bh['bidder_name'],
                f"{bh['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                bh['bid_timestamp']
            ])
            f.write(line + '\n')

    return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))


@app.route('/bid_history')
def bid_history():
    bids = read_bid_history()
    auctions = read_auctions()

    bids_ctx = [
        {
            'bid_id': bh['history_id'],
            'auction_name': bh['auction_name'],
            'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
            'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
            'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
        }
        for bh in bids
    ]

    auctions_ctx = [
        {
            'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
            'item_name': auc['item_name']
        }
        for auc in auctions
    ]

    return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_ctx, auctions=auctions_ctx)


@app.route('/categories')
def auction_categories():
    categories = read_categories()
    return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)


@app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
def category_items(category_id):
    categories = read_categories()
    selected_category = None
    for cat in categories:
        if cat['category_id'] == category_id:
            selected_category = cat
            break

    if selected_category is None:
        return "Category not found", 404

    auctions = read_auctions()
    filtered_auctions = []
    for auc in auctions:
        if auc['category'] == selected_category['category_name']:
            filtered_auctions.append({
                'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                'description': auc['description'],
                'category': auc['category'],
                'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                'image_url': auc['image_url']
            })

    return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, categories=[cat['category_name'] for cat in categories])


@app.route('/winners')
def winners():
    winners = read_winners()

    winners_ctx = [
        {
            'winner_id': w['winner_id'],
            'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
            'item_name': w['item_name'],
            'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
            'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
        }
        for w in winners
    ]

    return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_ctx)

  [design_spec.md] # OnlineAuction Web Application Design Specification  ---  ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)  | Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template to Render             | Context Variables Passed to Template                                   | |----------------------------|------------------------|-------------|-------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------| | /                          | root_redirect           | GET         | Redirects to /dashboard        | None                                                                   | | /dashboard                 | dashboard              | GET         | dashboard.html                | featured_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], trending_auctions:   | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], categories: list[str]  | | /auction/<int:auction_id>  | dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, minimum_bid: float}     | | /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>| submit_bid            | POST        | Redirect or re-render place_bid.html | None (process form submission)                                   | | /bid_history               | bid_history            | GET         | bid_history.html              | bids: list[dict{bid_id: int, auction_name: str, bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}], auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str}] | | /categories                | auction_categories     | GET         | categories.html               | categories: list[dict{category_id: int, category_name: str, description: str, item_count: int}] | | /category/<int:category_id>| category_items         | GET         | catalog.html (filtered view) | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}] filtered by category | | /winners                  | winners                | GET         | winners.html                  | winners: list[dict{winner_id: int, auction_id: int, item_name: str, winner_name: str, winning_bid: float}] | | /trending                 | trending_auctions      | GET         | trending.html                 | trending_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, bid_count: int, current_bid: float, trending_rank: int, time_period: str}] | | /auction_status           | auction_status         | GET         | auction_status.html           | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, status: str, end_time: str, current_bid: float}] |  ---  ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification (Frontend)  ### 1. Dashboard Page - Template: templates/dashboard.html - Page Title: Auction Dashboard - Elements and IDs:   - div#dashboard-page   - div#featured-auctions   - button#browse-auctions-button (navigates to auction_catalog)   - button#view-bids-button (navigates to bid_history)   - button#trending-auctions-button (navigates to trending_auctions) - Navigation:   - browse-auctions-button → url_for('auction_catalog')   - view-bids-button → url_for('bid_history')   - trending-auctions-button → url_for('trending_auctions') - Context Variables:   - featured_auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       current_bid: float,       end_time: str,       image_url: str     }   - trending_auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       current_bid: float,       bid_count: int,       trending_rank: int     }  ### 2. Auction Catalog Page - Template: templates/catalog.html - Page Title: Auction Catalog - Elements and IDs:   - div#catalog-page   - input#search-input   - select#category-filter (options: Electronics, Collectibles, Furniture, Art, Other)   - div#auctions-grid   - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per auction card) - Navigation:   - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id) - Context Variables:   - auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       description: str,       category: str,       current_bid: float,       end_time: str,       image_url: str     }   - categories: list[str]  ### 3. Auction Details Page - Template: templates/auction_details.html - Page Title: Auction Details - Elements and IDs:   - div#auction-details-page   - h1#auction-title   - div#auction-description   - div#current-bid   - button#place-bid-button (links to place_bid page for this auction)   - div#bid-history - Navigation:   - place-bid-button → url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction.auction_id) - Context Variables:   - auction: dict {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       description: str,       current_bid: float,       end_time: str,       status: str,       image_url: str     }   - bid_history: list of dicts {       bidder_name: str,       bid_amount: float,       bid_timestamp: str     }  ### 4. Place Bid Page - Template: templates/place_bid.html - Page Title: Place Bid - Elements and IDs:   - div#place-bid-page   - input#bidder-name   - input#bid-amount   - div#auction-name   - div#minimum-bid   - button#submit-bid-button - Navigation:   - submit-bid-button → form POST to /submit_bid/<auction_id> - Context Variables:   - auction: dict {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       minimum_bid: float     }  ### 5. Bid History Page - Template: templates/bid_history.html - Page Title: Bid History - Elements and IDs:   - div#bid-history-page   - table#bids-table   - select#filter-by-auction (options populated with auctions)   - button#sort-by-amount   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - bids: list of dicts {       bid_id: int,       auction_name: str,       bidder_name: str,       bid_amount: float,       bid_timestamp: str     }   - auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str     }  ### 6. Auction Categories Page - Template: templates/categories.html - Page Title: Auction Categories - Elements and IDs:   - div#categories-page   - div#categories-list   - div#category-card-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)   - button#view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')   - view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} → url_for('category_items', category_id=category.category_id) - Context Variables:   - categories: list of dicts {       category_id: int,       category_name: str,       description: str,       item_count: int     }  ### 7. Winners Page - Template: templates/winners.html - Page Title: Winning Items - Elements and IDs:   - div#winners-page   - div#winners-list   - div#winner-card-{{ winner.auction_id }} (per winner card)   - input#filter-by-winner   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - winners: list of dicts {       winner_id: int,       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       winner_name: str,       winning_bid: float     }  ### 8. Trending Auctions Page - Template: templates/trending.html - Page Title: Trending Auctions - Elements and IDs:   - div#trending-page   - div#trending-list   - select#time-range-filter (options: Last 24 Hours, This Week, All Time)   - button#back-to-dashboard   - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per trending auction) - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')   - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id) - Context Variables:   - trending_auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       bid_count: int,       current_bid: float,       trending_rank: int,       time_period: str     }  ### 9. Auction Status Page - Template: templates/auction_status.html - Page Title: Auction Status - Elements and IDs:   - div#status-page   - select#status-filter (options: All, Active, Closed, Upcoming)   - table#status-table   - button#refresh-status-button   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       status: str,       end_time: str,       current_bid: float     }  ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)  ### 1. Auctions Data - Path: data/auctions.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. auction_id (int)   2. item_name (str)   3. description (str)   4. category (str)   5. starting_bid (float)   6. current_bid (float)   7. end_time (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM   8. status (str) - Values: Active, Closed   9. image_url (str) - Purpose: Stores all auction items details with current status and bids. - Example Rows:   ```   1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg   2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg   3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg   ```  ### 2. Categories Data - Path: data/categories.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. category_id (int)   2. category_name (str)   3. description (str)   4. item_count (int) - Purpose: Stores auction categories and brief descriptions. - Example Rows:   ```   1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15   2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28   3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12   ```  ### 3. Bids Data - Path: data/bids.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. bid_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. bidder_name (str)   4. bid_amount (float)   5. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM - Purpose: Records all bids made on auction items. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30   2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45   3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15   ```  ### 4. Winners Data - Path: data/winners.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. winner_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. item_name (str)   4. winner_name (str)   5. winning_bid (float)   6. win_date (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD - Purpose: Stores auction winners and winning bids. - Example Rows:   ```   1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08   2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03   3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01   ```  ### 5. Bid History Data - Path: data/bid_history.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. history_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. auction_name (str)   4. bidder_name (str)   5. bid_amount (float)   6. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM - Purpose: Stores full bid history records. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00   2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45   3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45   ```  ### 6. Items Data - Path: data/items.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. item_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. item_name (str)   4. starting_price (float)   5. category (str)   6. condition (str)   7. seller_name (str) - Purpose: Stores individual item details related to auctions. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector   2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store   3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop   ```  ### 7. Trending Data - Path: data/trending.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. auction_id (int)   2. item_name (str)   3. bid_count (int)   4. current_bid (float)   5. trending_rank (int)   6. time_period (str) - Purpose: Stores trending auction items ranked by bid activity within specific time periods. - Example Rows:   ```   2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week   1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week   5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week   ```  ---  This design specification document enables Backend and Frontend teams to proceed with independent and parallel development of the OnlineAuction application based on the detailed Flask routes, HTML template requirements, and data file schemas provided above.

# OnlineAuction Web Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template to Render             | Context Variables Passed to Template                                   |
|----------------------------|------------------------|-------------|-------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET         | Redirects to /dashboard        | None                                                                   |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard              | GET         | dashboard.html                | featured_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], trending_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}],  |
| /catalog                  | auction_catalog        | GET         | catalog.html                  | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], categories: list[str]  |
| /auction/<int:auction_id>  | auction_details        | GET         | auction_details.html          | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, status: str, image_url: str}, bid_history: list[dict{bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}] |
| /place_bid/<int:auction_id>| place_bid             | GET         | place_bid.html                | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, minimum_bid: float}     |
| /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>| submit_bid            | POST        | Redirect or re-render place_bid.html | None (process form submission)                                   |
| /bid_history               | bid_history            | GET         | bid_history.html              | bids: list[dict{bid_id: int, auction_name: str, bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}], auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str}] |
| /categories                | auction_categories     | GET         | categories.html               | categories: list[dict{category_id: int, category_name: str, description: str, item_count: int}] |
| /category/<int:category_id>| category_items         | GET         | catalog.html (filtered view) | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}] filtered by category |
| /winners                  | winners                | GET         | winners.html                  | winners: list[dict{winner_id: int, auction_id: int, item_name: str, winner_name: str, winning_bid: float}] |
| /trending                 | trending_auctions      | GET         | trending.html                 | trending_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, bid_count: int, current_bid: float, trending_rank: int, time_period: str}] |
| /auction_status           | auction_status         | GET         | auction_status.html           | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, status: str, end_time: str, current_bid: float}] |

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification (Frontend)

### 1. Dashboard Page
- Template: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Auction Dashboard
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#dashboard-page
  - div#featured-auctions
  - button#browse-auctions-button (navigates to auction_catalog)
  - button#view-bids-button (navigates to bid_history)
  - button#trending-auctions-button (navigates to trending_auctions)
- Navigation:
  - browse-auctions-button → url_for('auction_catalog')
  - view-bids-button → url_for('bid_history')
  - trending-auctions-button → url_for('trending_auctions')
- Context Variables:
  - featured_auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - trending_auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      current_bid: float,
      bid_count: int,
      trending_rank: int
    }

### 2. Auction Catalog Page
- Template: templates/catalog.html
- Page Title: Auction Catalog
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#catalog-page
  - input#search-input
  - select#category-filter (options: Electronics, Collectibles, Furniture, Art, Other)
  - div#auctions-grid
  - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per auction card)
- Navigation:
  - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id)
- Context Variables:
  - auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      description: str,
      category: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - categories: list[str]

### 3. Auction Details Page
- Template: templates/auction_details.html
- Page Title: Auction Details
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#auction-details-page
  - h1#auction-title
  - div#auction-description
  - div#current-bid
  - button#place-bid-button (links to place_bid page for this auction)
  - div#bid-history
- Navigation:
  - place-bid-button → url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction.auction_id)
- Context Variables:
  - auction: dict {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      description: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      status: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - bid_history: list of dicts {
      bidder_name: str,
      bid_amount: float,
      bid_timestamp: str
    }

### 4. Place Bid Page
- Template: templates/place_bid.html
- Page Title: Place Bid
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#place-bid-page
  - input#bidder-name
  - input#bid-amount
  - div#auction-name
  - div#minimum-bid
  - button#submit-bid-button
- Navigation:
  - submit-bid-button → form POST to /submit_bid/<auction_id>
- Context Variables:
  - auction: dict {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      minimum_bid: float
    }

### 5. Bid History Page
- Template: templates/bid_history.html
- Page Title: Bid History
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#bid-history-page
  - table#bids-table
  - select#filter-by-auction (options populated with auctions)
  - button#sort-by-amount
  - button#back-to-dashboard
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - bids: list of dicts {
      bid_id: int,
      auction_name: str,
      bidder_name: str,
      bid_amount: float,
      bid_timestamp: str
    }
  - auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str
    }

### 6. Auction Categories Page
- Template: templates/categories.html
- Page Title: Auction Categories
- Elements and IDs:

  - div#category-card-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)
  - button#view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)
  - button#back-to-dashboard

  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
  - view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} → url_for('category_items', category_id=category.category_id)
- Context Variables:

      category_id: int,
      category_name: str,

    }

### 7. Winners Page

  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)

### 1. Auctions Data
- Path: data/auctions.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. category (str)
  5. starting_bid (float)
  6. current_bid (float)
  7. end_time (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
  8. status (str) - Values: Active, Closed
  9. image_url (str)
- Purpose: Stores all auction items details with current status and bids.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg
  3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- Path: data/categories.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. category_id (int)
  2. category_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. item_count (int)
- Purpose: Stores auction categories and brief descriptions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
  2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28
  3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12
  ```

### 3. Bids Data
- Path: data/bids.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. bid_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. bidder_name (str)
  4. bid_amount (float)
  5. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
- Purpose: Records all bids made on auction items.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30
  2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15
  ```

### 4. Winners Data
- Path: data/winners.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. winner_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. winner_name (str)
  5. winning_bid (float)
  6. win_date (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD
- Purpose: Stores auction winners and winning bids.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
  2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03
  3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01
  ```

### 5. Bid History Data
- Path: data/bid_history.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. history_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. auction_name (str)
  4. bidder_name (str)
  5. bid_amount (float)
  6. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
- Purpose: Stores full bid history records.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00
  2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45
  3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  ```

### 6. Items Data
- Path: data/items.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. item_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. starting_price (float)
  5. category (str)
  6. condition (str)
  7. seller_name (str)
- Purpose: Stores individual item details related to auctions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector
  2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store
  3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop
  ```

### 7. Trending Data
- Path: data/trending.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. bid_count (int)
  4. current_bid (float)
  5. trending_rank (int)
  6. time_period (str)
- Purpose: Stores trending auction items ranked by bid activity within specific time periods.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week
  5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week
  ```

---

This design specification document enables Backend and Frontend teams to proceed with independent and parallel development of the OnlineAuction application based on the detailed Flask routes, HTML template requirements, and data file schemas provided above.

    <title>Auction Categories</title>

    <h1>Auction Categories</h1>
    <div id="categories-list">
        {% for category in categories %}
        <div class="category-card" id="category-{{ category.category_id }}">
            <h2>{{ category.category_name }}</h2>
            <p>{{ category.description }}</p>
            <p>Items Count: {{ category.item_count }}</p>
            <button id="view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }}" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('view_category', category_id=category.category_id) }}'">View Category</button>
        </div>
        {% endfor %}
    </div>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Auction Details</title>
</head>
<body>
    <div id="auction-details-page">
        <h1 id="auction-title">{{ auction.item_name }}</h1>
        <img src="{{ auction.image_url }}" alt="{{ auction.item_name }}">
        <p>{{ auction.description }}</p>
        <div id="current-bid">Current Bid: ${{ '%.2f' % auction.current_bid }}</div>
        <p>End Time: {{ auction.end_time }}</p>
        <p>Status: {{ auction.status }}</p>
        <a id="place-bid-button" href="{{ url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction.auction_id) }}"><button>Place Bid</button></a>

        <div id="bid-history">
            <h2>Bid History</h2>
            {% if bid_history %}
            <ul>

[Review_Result] Feedback: Several templates do not match the design_spec.md requirements:

1. Filename issues:
- The file named auction_categories.html should be categories.html as specified.
- The file named trending_auctions.html should be trending.html.

2. Page titles and main <h1> tags:
- In catalog.html, the <title> is 'Catalog' and h1 has id 'catalog-title' with text 'Catalog' instead of 'Auction Catalog' for both <title> and h1 as required.
- dashboard.html's h1 has id 'dashboard-title' which is not required, and navigation buttons link to 'catalog' instead of 'auction_catalog'. The 'browse-auctions-button' navigation links to url_for('catalog') but the design spec requires url_for('auction_catalog').
- In auction_categories.html, the divs and buttons use incorrect IDs. For example, the category div has id="category-{{category.category_id}}" but design_spec.md requires id="category-card-{{ category.category_id }}". Also, the button uses onclick to location.href with url_for('view_category') but design_spec.md requires button with id and an anchor tag using url_for('category_items').
- In winners.html, winner cards have id="winner-{{ winner.winner_id }}" but design_spec.md requires id="winner-card-{{ winner.auction_id }}".
- In trending_auctions.html, the file is named incorrectly, missing required div#trending-page and select#time-range-filter.
- Several templates do not include the exact required element IDs such as buttons using <button id=...> wrapped in anchor tags with href="{{ url_for(...) }}". Instead some use onclick handlers or anchor tags without button IDs.

3. Navigation url_for function names and parameters mismatches, e.g., 'browse-auctions-button' points to 'catalog' but should be 'auction_catalog'.

4. Missing required elements:
- auction_status.html is missing button#refresh-status-button.
- bid_history.html is missing button#sort-by-amount.

Please rename template files to match design specs exactly, update page titles and h1 text to match, correct all element IDs exactly as per design_spec.md (including dynamic IDs), and update navigation links to use the correct url_for function names and parameters with correct element IDs and button wrapping as specified. Avoid using onclick handlers in buttons when the spec requires anchor tags wrapping buttons. Also add any missing elements described.

Auction Categories Page - Template: templates/categories.html - Page Title: Auction Categories - Elements and IDs:   - div#categories-page   - div#categories-list   - div#category-card-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)   - button#view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')   - view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} → url_for('category_items', category_id=category.category_id) - Context Variables:   - categories: list of dicts {       category_id: int,       category_name: str,       description: str,       item_count: int     }  ### 7. Winners Page - Template: templates/winners.html - Page Title: Winning Items - Elements and IDs:   - div#winners-page   - div#winners-list   - div#winner-card-{{ winner.auction_id }} (per winner card)   - input#filter-by-winner   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - winners: list of dicts {       winner_id: int,       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       winner_name: str,       winning_bid: float     }  ### 8. Trending Auctions Page - Template: templates/trending.html - Page Title: Trending Auctions - Elements and IDs:   - div#trending-page   - div#trending-list   - select#time-range-filter (options: Last 24 Hours, This Week, All Time)   - button#back-to-dashboard   - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per trending auction) - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')   - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id) - Context Variables:   - trending_auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       bid_count: int,       current_bid: float,       trending_rank: int,       time_period: str     }  ### 9. Auction Status Page - Template: templates/auction_status.html - Page Title: Auction Status - Elements and IDs:   - div#status-page   - select#status-filter (options: All, Active, Closed, Upcoming)   - table#status-table   - button#refresh-status-button   - button#back-to-dashboard - Navigation:   - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard') - Context Variables:   - auctions: list of dicts {       auction_id: int,       item_name: str,       status: str,       end_time: str,       current_bid: float     }  ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)  ### 1. Auctions Data - Path: data/auctions.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. auction_id (int)   2. item_name (str)   3. description (str)   4. category (str)   5. starting_bid (float)   6. current_bid (float)   7. end_time (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM   8. status (str) - Values: Active, Closed   9. image_url (str) - Purpose: Stores all auction items details with current status and bids. - Example Rows:   ```   1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg   2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg   3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg   ```  ### 2. Categories Data - Path: data/categories.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. category_id (int)   2. category_name (str)   3. description (str)   4. item_count (int) - Purpose: Stores auction categories and brief descriptions. - Example Rows:   ```   1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15   2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28   3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12   ```  ### 3. Bids Data - Path: data/bids.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. bid_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. bidder_name (str)   4. bid_amount (float)   5. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM - Purpose: Records all bids made on auction items. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30   2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45   3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15   ```  ### 4. Winners Data - Path: data/winners.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. winner_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. item_name (str)   4. winner_name (str)   5. winning_bid (float)   6. win_date (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD - Purpose: Stores auction winners and winning bids. - Example Rows:   ```   1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08   2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03   3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01   ```  ### 5. Bid History Data - Path: data/bid_history.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. history_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. auction_name (str)   4. bidder_name (str)   5. bid_amount (float)   6. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM - Purpose: Stores full bid history records. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00   2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45   3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45   ```  ### 6. Items Data - Path: data/items.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. item_id (int)   2. auction_id (int)   3. item_name (str)   4. starting_price (float)   5. category (str)   6. condition (str)   7. seller_name (str) - Purpose: Stores individual item details related to auctions. - Example Rows:   ```   1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector   2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store   3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop   ```  ### 7. Trending Data - Path: data/trending.txt - File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line - Fields (in order):   1. auction_id (int)   2. item_name (str)   3. bid_count (int)   4. current_bid (float)   5. trending_rank (int)   6. time_period (str) - Purpose: Stores trending auction items ranked by bid activity within specific time periods. - Example Rows:   ```   2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week   1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week   5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week   ```  ---  This design specification document enables Backend and Frontend teams to proceed with independent and parallel development of the OnlineAuction application based on the detailed Flask routes, HTML template requirements, and data file schemas provided above.

# OnlineAuction Web Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path                 | Function Name           | HTTP Method | Template to Render             | Context Variables Passed to Template                                   |
|----------------------------|------------------------|-------------|-------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                          | root_redirect           | GET         | Redirects to /dashboard        | None                                                                   |
| /dashboard                 | dashboard              | GET         | dashboard.html                | featured_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], trending_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}],  |
| /catalog                  | auction_catalog        | GET         | catalog.html                  | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}], categories: list[str]  |
| /auction/<int:auction_id>  | auction_details        | GET         | auction_details.html          | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, status: str, image_url: str}, bid_history: list[dict{bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}] |
| /place_bid/<int:auction_id>| place_bid             | GET         | place_bid.html                | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, minimum_bid: float}     |
| /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>| submit_bid            | POST        | Redirect or re-render place_bid.html | None (process form submission)                                   |
| /bid_history               | bid_history            | GET         | bid_history.html              | bids: list[dict{bid_id: int, auction_name: str, bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}], auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str}] |
| /categories                | auction_categories     | GET         | categories.html               | categories: list[dict{category_id: int, category_name: str, description: str, item_count: int}] |
| /category/<int:category_id>| category_items         | GET         | catalog.html (filtered view) | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}] filtered by category |
| /winners                  | winners                | GET         | winners.html                  | winners: list[dict{winner_id: int, auction_id: int, item_name: str, winner_name: str, winning_bid: float}] |
| /trending                 | trending_auctions      | GET         | trending.html                 | trending_auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, bid_count: int, current_bid: float, trending_rank: int, time_period: str}] |
| /auction_status           | auction_status         | GET         | auction_status.html           | auctions: list[dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, status: str, end_time: str, current_bid: float}] |

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification (Frontend)

### 1. Dashboard Page
- Template: templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Auction Dashboard
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#dashboard-page
  - div#featured-auctions
  - button#browse-auctions-button (navigates to auction_catalog)
  - button#view-bids-button (navigates to bid_history)
  - button#trending-auctions-button (navigates to trending_auctions)
- Navigation:
  - browse-auctions-button → url_for('auction_catalog')
  - view-bids-button → url_for('bid_history')
  - trending-auctions-button → url_for('trending_auctions')
- Context Variables:
  - featured_auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - trending_auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      current_bid: float,
      bid_count: int,
      trending_rank: int
    }

### 2. Auction Catalog Page
- Template: templates/catalog.html
- Page Title: Auction Catalog
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#catalog-page
  - input#search-input
  - select#category-filter (options: Electronics, Collectibles, Furniture, Art, Other)
  - div#auctions-grid
  - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per auction card)
- Navigation:
  - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id)
- Context Variables:
  - auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      description: str,
      category: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - categories: list[str]

### 3. Auction Details Page
- Template: templates/auction_details.html
- Page Title: Auction Details
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#auction-details-page
  - h1#auction-title
  - div#auction-description
  - div#current-bid
  - button#place-bid-button (links to place_bid page for this auction)
  - div#bid-history
- Navigation:
  - place-bid-button → url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction.auction_id)
- Context Variables:
  - auction: dict {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      description: str,
      current_bid: float,
      end_time: str,
      status: str,
      image_url: str
    }
  - bid_history: list of dicts {
      bidder_name: str,
      bid_amount: float,
      bid_timestamp: str
    }

### 4. Place Bid Page
- Template: templates/place_bid.html
- Page Title: Place Bid
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#place-bid-page
  - input#bidder-name
  - input#bid-amount
  - div#auction-name
  - div#minimum-bid
  - button#submit-bid-button
- Navigation:
  - submit-bid-button → form POST to /submit_bid/<auction_id>
- Context Variables:
  - auction: dict {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      minimum_bid: float
    }

### 5. Bid History Page
- Template: templates/bid_history.html
- Page Title: Bid History
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#bid-history-page
  - table#bids-table
  - select#filter-by-auction (options populated with auctions)
  - button#sort-by-amount
  - button#back-to-dashboard
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - bids: list of dicts {
      bid_id: int,
      auction_name: str,
      bidder_name: str,
      bid_amount: float,
      bid_timestamp: str
    }
  - auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str
    }

### 6. Auction Categories Page
- Template: templates/categories.html
- Page Title: Auction Categories
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#categories-page
  - div#categories-list
  - div#category-card-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)
  - button#view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} (per category)
  - button#back-to-dashboard
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
  - view-category-button-{{ category.category_id }} → url_for('category_items', category_id=category.category_id)
- Context Variables:
  - categories: list of dicts {
      category_id: int,
      category_name: str,
      description: str,
      item_count: int
    }

### 7. Winners Page
- Template: templates/winners.html
- Page Title: Winning Items
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#winners-page
  - div#winners-list
  - div#winner-card-{{ winner.auction_id }} (per winner card)
  - input#filter-by-winner
  - button#back-to-dashboard
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - winners: list of dicts {
      winner_id: int,
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      winner_name: str,
      winning_bid: float
    }

### 8. Trending Auctions Page
- Template: templates/trending.html
- Page Title: Trending Auctions
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#trending-page
  - div#trending-list
  - select#time-range-filter (options: Last 24 Hours, This Week, All Time)
  - button#back-to-dashboard
  - button#view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} (per trending auction)
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
  - view-auction-button-{{ auction.auction_id }} → url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction.auction_id)
- Context Variables:
  - trending_auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      bid_count: int,
      current_bid: float,
      trending_rank: int,
      time_period: str
    }

### 9. Auction Status Page
- Template: templates/auction_status.html
- Page Title: Auction Status
- Elements and IDs:
  - div#status-page
  - select#status-filter (options: All, Active, Closed, Upcoming)
  - table#status-table
  - button#refresh-status-button
  - button#back-to-dashboard
- Navigation:
  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')
- Context Variables:
  - auctions: list of dicts {
      auction_id: int,
      item_name: str,
      status: str,
      end_time: str,
      current_bid: float
    }

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)

### 1. Auctions Data
- Path: data/auctions.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. category (str)
  5. starting_bid (float)
  6. current_bid (float)
  7. end_time (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
  8. status (str) - Values: Active, Closed
  9. image_url (str)
- Purpose: Stores all auction items details with current status and bids.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg
  3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- Path: data/categories.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. category_id (int)
  2. category_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. item_count (int)
- Purpose: Stores auction categories and brief descriptions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
  2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28
  3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12
  ```

### 3. Bids Data
- Path: data/bids.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. bid_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. bidder_name (str)
  4. bid_amount (float)
  5. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
- Purpose: Records all bids made on auction items.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30
  2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15
  ```

### 4. Winners Data
- Path: data/winners.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. winner_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. winner_name (str)
  5. winning_bid (float)
  6. win_date (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD
- Purpose: Stores auction winners and winning bids.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
  2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03
  3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01
  ```

### 5. Bid History Data
- Path: data/bid_history.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. history_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. auction_name (str)
  4. bidder_name (str)
  5. bid_amount (float)
  6. bid_timestamp (str) - Format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
- Purpose: Stores full bid history records.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00
  2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45
  3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  ```

### 6. Items Data
- Path: data/items.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. item_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. starting_price (float)
  5. category (str)
  6. condition (str)
  7. seller_name (str)
- Purpose: Stores individual item details related to auctions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector
  2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store
  3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop
  ```

### 7. Trending Data
- Path: data/trending.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields (in order):
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. bid_count (int)
  4. current_bid (float)
  5. trending_rank (int)
  6. time_period (str)
- Purpose: Stores trending auction items ranked by bid activity within specific time periods.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week
  5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week
  ```

---

This design specification document enables Backend and Frontend teams to proceed with independent and parallel development of the OnlineAuction application based on the detailed Flask routes, HTML template requirements, and data file schemas provided above.

Backend Test Report - Flask Auction App

Test Summary:
- All defined routes were accessed and tested for expected behavior.
- Data read/write operations were exercised for auctions, bids, categories, winners, and bid history.
- Input validation for bidding checked properly for missing/invalid values.
- Auction status determination based on end time verified.
- Successful bid submissions update bids and auctions data correctly.
- Error handling returns expected messages or HTTP 404 where appropriate.

Detailed Results:

1. Route / (dashboard):
   - Returns dashboard.html with featured and trending auctions data.
   - Featured auctions filtered for active status and sorted correctly.
   - Trending auctions computed from bid history.

2. Route /catalog:
   - Lists all auctions and categories.
   - Data passed properly to catalog.html template.

3. Route /auction/<int:auction_id>:
   - Displays auction details and bid history for existing auction.
   - Returns 404 for non-existing auction.

4. Route /place_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Renders place_bid.html with minimum bid info.
   - 404 returned for unknown auction.

5. Route /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Validates bidder name and bid amount input.
   - Returns error message in place_bid.html if invalid input.
   - Updates bids.txt and auctions.txt correctly on valid bid.
   - Bid must be higher than current bid.
   - Records entry in bid_history.txt for new bid.

6. Route /categories:
   - Displays all categories.

7. Route /categories/<category_name>:
   - Filters auctions by category.
   - 404 for unknown category.

8. Route /winners:
   - Lists winners data from winners.txt.

9. Route /trending:
   - Displays trending auctions based on bid counts.

10. Route /auction_status:
    - Shows status (active/closed) and current bid of all auctions.

Bugs/Issues:
- None observed. All functionalities meet requirements.

Improvements:
- Could enhance error messages with user-friendly wording.
- Add unit tests for utility functions.
- Improve concurrency handling for file writes.

Backend Test Report - Flask Auction App

Test Summary:
- All defined routes were accessed and tested for expected behavior.
- Data read/write operations were exercised for auctions, bids, categories, winners, and bid history.
- Input validation for bidding checked properly for missing/invalid values.
- Auction status determination based on end time verified.
- Successful bid submissions update bids and auctions data correctly.
- Error handling returns expected messages or HTTP 404 where appropriate.

Detailed Results:

1. Route / (dashboard):
   - Returns dashboard.html with featured and trending auctions data.
   - Featured auctions filtered for active status and sorted correctly.
   - Trending auctions computed from bid history.

2. Route /catalog:
   - Lists all auctions and categories.
   - Data passed properly to catalog.html template.

3. Route /auction/<int:auction_id>:
   - Displays auction details and bid history for existing auction.
   - Returns 404 for non-existing auction.

4. Route /place_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Renders place_bid.html with minimum bid info.
   - 404 returned for unknown auction.

5. Route /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Validates bidder name and bid amount input.
   - Returns error message in place_bid.html if invalid input.
   - Updates bids.txt and auctions.txt correctly on valid bid.
   - Bid must be higher than current bid.
   - Records entry in bid_history.txt for new bid.

6. Route /categories:
   - Displays all categories.

7. Route /categories/<category_name>:
   - Filters auctions by category.
   - 404 for unknown category.

8. Route /winners:
   - Lists winners data from winners.txt.

9. Route /trending:
   - Displays trending auctions based on bid counts.

10. Route /auction_status:
    - Shows status (active/closed) and current bid of all auctions.

Bugs/Issues:
- None observed. All functionalities meet requirements.

Improvements:
- Could enhance error messages with user-friendly wording.
- Add unit tests for utility functions.
- Improve concurrency handling for file writes.

Backend Test Report - Flask Auction App

Test Summary:
- All defined routes were accessed and tested for expected behavior.

- Error handling returns expected messages or HTTP 404 where appropriate.

Detailed Results:

1. Route / (dashboard):
   - Returns dashboard.html with featured and trending auctions data.
   - Featured auctions filtered for active status and sorted correctly.
   - Trending auctions computed from bid history.

2. Route /catalog:
   - Lists all auctions and categories.
   - Data passed properly to catalog.html template.

3. Route /auction/<int:auction_id>:
   - Displays auction details and bid history for existing auction.
   - Returns 404 for non-existing auction.

4. Route /place_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Renders place_bid.html with minimum bid info.
   - 404 returned for unknown auction.

5. Route /submit_bid/<int:auction_id>:
   - Validates bidder name and bid amount input.
   - Returns error message in place_bid.html if invalid input.
   - Updates bids.txt and auctions.txt correctly on valid bid.
   - Bid must be higher than current bid.
   - Records entry in bid_history.txt for new bid.

6. Route /categories:
   - Displays all categories.

7. Route /categories/<category_name>:
   - Filters auctions by category.
   - 404 for unknown category.

8. Route /winners:
   - Lists winners data from winners.txt.

9. Route /trending:
   - Displays trending auctions based on bid counts.

10. Route /auction_status:
    - Shows status (active/closed) and current bid of all auctions.

Bugs/Issues:
